<div>   
<input type="hidden" id="topicId" value="1128462">
<input type="hidden" value id="puid">


<div class="abstract">
<p>「高能电玩节」正式开始了。</p>
</div>

                
<div class="topicContent front_content"><p>　　作为「高能电玩节」的一环，B 站举办的「高能独立游戏夜」在今天带来 30 余款独立游戏的首发情报，诸如《沙石镇时光》《光明记忆：无限》《天命奇御2》《纪元：变异》《仙剑奇侠传七》等游戏在发布会上亮相。</p><p>　　我们为大家做了发布会游戏新情报汇总。</p><p>　　<a href="https://www.bilibili.com/video/BV1oh411h7Kb?share_source=copy_web">发布会全程视频</a>：</p><div class="vg_insert_video"><figure contenteditable="false"><iframe class="vg_insert_video_iframe new_bilibili" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen src="https://player.bilibili.com/player.html?aid=206555423&bvid=BV1oh411h7Kb&cid=366375402&page=1" height="513"></iframe><figcaption contenteditable="true" class="vg_insert_video_notice"></figcaption></figure><div class="vg_insert_video_cover bili_cover bili_cover_new" contenteditable="false" style="height:513px"><b class="bili_play"></b><span class="vg_insert_video_del" contenteditable="false"></span></div></div><hr class="vg_hr" contenteditable="false"><p><b>《光明记忆 无限》最新预告</b></p><div class="vg_insert_video"><figure contenteditable="false"><iframe class="vg_insert_video_iframe new_bilibili" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen src="https://player.bilibili.com/player.html?aid=931504912&bvid=BV1jM4y1M7cD&cid=366404884&page=1" height="513"></iframe><figcaption contenteditable="true" class="vg_insert_video_notice"></figcaption></figure><div class="vg_insert_video_cover bili_cover bili_cover_new" contenteditable="false" style="height:513px"><b class="bili_play"></b><span class="vg_insert_video_del" contenteditable="false"></span></div></div><p style="text-align: right;"><a href="https://www.bilibili.com/video/BV1jM4y1M7cD?share_source=copy_web">视频地址</a></p><p><span style="background-color: initial; letter-spacing: 1.3px;">　　预告视频中展现了全新的武器和侗族鼓楼等战斗场景，并</span><span style="background-color: initial; letter-spacing: 1.3px;">展示了游戏后期的一段 BOSS 战，玩家与“天宇大帝”之前的神秘面具人在 2 万米高空的悬空寺中战斗，玩家通过飙车前往山顶，使用牵引器勾住失控的飞机前往这座被黑洞引力牵制的悬空城市中。</span></p><hr class="vg_hr" contenteditable="false"><p><b style="background-color: initial; letter-spacing: 1.3px;">　　<a href="https://www.bilibili.com/video/BV1r64y167GQ?share_source=copy_web">《斩妖行》</a>正式版于今日上线</b><br></p><p><span style="background-color: initial; letter-spacing: 1.3px;">　　正式版游戏增加了全新女主线，玩家可以选择成为白毛半妖“夏侯雪”，体会不一样的斩妖故事。</span><br></p><p align="left">　　游戏首月将维持抢先体验版的价格。之前购买了抢先体验版的玩家可免费更新至完整版，无需额外付费。</p><div class="vg_insert_video"><figure contenteditable="false"><iframe class="vg_insert_video_iframe new_bilibili" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen src="https://player.bilibili.com/player.html?aid=761012649&bvid=BV1r64y167GQ&cid=353716641&page=1" height="513"></iframe><figcaption contenteditable="true" class="vg_insert_video_notice"></figcaption></figure><div class="vg_insert_video_cover bili_cover bili_cover_new" contenteditable="false" style="height:513px"><b class="bili_play"></b><span class="vg_insert_video_del" contenteditable="false"></span></div></div><hr class="vg_hr" contenteditable="false"><p><b style="background-color: initial; letter-spacing: 1.3px;">《仙剑奇侠传七》光线追踪演示</b></p><p>　　演示展示了多个场景和人物在开启光线追踪后的效果。</p><p>　　软星科技表示，“<span style="letter-spacing: 1.3px;">光线追踪技术在《仙剑奇侠传七》的研发中得到了全面应用，帮助游戏提升了整体光线氛围的营造。</span><span style="background-color: initial; letter-spacing: 1.3px;">”</span></p><div class="vg_insert_video"><figure contenteditable="false"><iframe class="vg_insert_video_iframe new_bilibili" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen src="https://player.bilibili.com/player.html?aid=889041674&bvid=BV1yK4y1M7v7&cid=366329490&page=1" height="513"></iframe><figcaption contenteditable="true" class="vg_insert_video_notice"></figcaption></figure><div class="vg_insert_video_cover bili_cover bili_cover_new" contenteditable="false" style="height:513px"><b class="bili_play"></b><span class="vg_insert_video_del" contenteditable="false"></span></div></div><p style="text-align: right;"><a href="https://www.bilibili.com/video/BV1yK4y1M7v7?share_source=copy_web">视频地址</a></p>
